data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;a class="_58cn" href="/hashtag/opinion?source=feed_text&amp;story_id=899701270094270" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;*N&quot;,&quot;type&quot;:104&#125;"&gt;&lt;span aria-label="hashtag" class="_58cl"&gt;#&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="_58cm"&gt;OPINION&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt; : Daniel Gros (Director of the Brussels-based Center for European Policy Studies)  :Saving &lt;a class="_58cn" href="/hashtag/greece?source=feed_text&amp;story_id=899701270094270" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;*N&quot;,&quot;type&quot;:104&#125;"&gt;&lt;span aria-label="hashtag" class="_58cl"&gt;#&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="_58cm"&gt;Greece&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt; was always going to be difficult, given its previous fiscal excesses and weak economy. But last year, it seemed that success was within reach  until the clash of narratives derailed the progress the two sides had made. This highlights a larger problem: the &lt;a class="_58cn" href="/hashtag/eu?source=feed_text&amp;story_id=899701270094270" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;*N&quot;,&quot;type&quot;:104&#125;"&gt;&lt;span aria-label="hashtag" class="_58cl"&gt;#&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="_58cm"&gt;EU&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt; lacks a unifying narrative strong enough to prevent the emergence of conflicting  and highly destructive  narratives within its borders. In this sense, the failure to save Greece amounts to a failure of Europe.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;H&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;div class="mtm"&gt;&lt;div David passed away in February 2014. His last words were &#x201c;tempus fugit&#x201d; (time is escaping).
